  "SummaryOfFindings": "The project is a three-tier network visualization tool with a React frontend, a Hono/Bun backend, and a Go-based data collector. The architecture is mostly sound but reveals several inconsistencies and incomplete features.\n\n**Key Findings:**\n1.  **Architecture:** The `frontend`, `server`, `database`, and `cache` are designed to run together via `docker-compose`. The `collector` is a standalone agent that pushes data to the server API, but its integration into the development environment is not defined, complicating local testing.\n2.  **Incomplete Core Feature:** The most significant issue is that the `collector` uses a hardcoded device list. The functionality to dynamically add and manage monitored devices from the main application appears to be unimplemented.\n3.  **Deployment Issues:**\n    *   The `collector` is configured to contact the API at `localhost`, which will fail in a containerized environment where services should be reached via their service names.\n    *   The `server`'s Docker image is not optimized with a multi-stage build, leading to a larger-than-necessary image size.\n    *   A default JWT secret is used in the `docker-compose.yml`, which is a security risk for production.\n4.  **Code Quality:** The project uses modern technologies like Bun, Hono, and Drizzle, with good practices like API documentation (`swagger-ui`) and validation (`zod`).
